            production induced by neutrons with energies between  2272400100004 
            28 and 63 MeV incident energies on oxygen             2272400100005 
AUTHOR     (S.Benck, I.Slypen, J.P.Meulders, V.Corcalciuc)        2272400100006 
INSTITUTE  (2BLGLVN)  Institut de Physique Nucleaire, Universitee 2272400100007

REFERENCE  (J,AND,72,1,1999)   Main reference, full data tables   2272400100012

           (J,EPJ/A,3,149,1998)   Data for H-1, H-2, graphs       2272400100014

FACILITY   (CYCLO,2BLGLVN)  Fast neutron facility of the Louvain- 2272400100017

INC-SOURCE (P-LI7)   The 65-MeV incident proton beam is focused   2272400100019 
              on a 3-mm-thick natural lithium target. With a beam 2272400100020 
             intensity of 10.E-5 A, about 10E+6 neutrons/s are    2272400100021 
             available at the location of reaction chamber (about 2272400100022 
             3.3 m downstream of the lithium target).             2272400100023 
INC-SPECT  .The neutron energy spectrum at zero degree consists   2272400100024 
            of a well-defined peak (2 MeV full-width-at-half-     2272400100025 
            maximum) containing about 50% of the neutrons, plus   2272400100026 
            a flat continuum of lower energy neutrons             2272400100027 
DETECTOR   (TELES,SCIN,CSICR) Four charged particle detector      2272400100028 
             telescopes were used simultaneously. Each of them    2272400100029 
             consists of DE detector (NE102 plastic scintillator) 2272400100030 
             and an E detector (CsI(Tl) crystal)                  2272400100031 
METHOD     (TOF)   Time-of-Flight                                 2272400100032 
           (COINC) Coincidence between E and DE detectors         2272400100033 
           (EDE)                                                  2272400100034 
           (SITA) Sucessive measurements of Al and Al2-O3 samples 2272400100035 
ANALYSIS   .Time-of-flight (TOF) signal between a capacitive beam 2272400100036 
            pickoff located upstream from the neutron producing   2272400100037 
            target and the DE detector is registered. This signal 2272400100038 
            is subsequently used to select only those events      2272400100039 
            associated with the incident neutrons in a desired    2272400100040 
            energy interval. The time resolution in the experiment2272400100041 
            was 0.8 ns [7].                                       2272400100042 
MONITOR    (1-H-1(N,EL)1-H-1,,SIG)  For energy calibration, the   2272400100043 
             protons and deuterons recoiling respectively from a  2272400100044 
             1-mm thick polypropylene and 0.6-mm thick deuterated 2272400100045 
             polypropylene target were used. The H(n,p) scattering2272400100046 
             is registered with good statistics, for a precise    2272400100047 
             determination of differential cross-sections to be   2272400100048 
             subsequently used as reference cross-sections.       2272400100049 
MONIT-REF  (,S.Benck+,J,NP/A,615,220,1997)                        2272400100050 
CORRECTION .Corrections were made on the sample thickness for     2272400100051 
            low energy charged particles                          2272400100052 
SAMPLE     .Elemental Al and Al2-O3, each 5*5 cm2 surface,        2272400100053 
            1 mm thick                                            2272400100054 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T)  Total error includes statistical and systema- 2272400100055 
                    ti errors                                     2272400100056
